 Anam Devi, a relative of Sona Devi, says doctors say we have to buy medicines from outside

 chathe bed par aashaa kumari hai, jo jald hi bachche ko janm dene vaali hai
 The Bihar government says that all patients admitted to rural hospitals are entitled to three to four meals a day
 aashaa kumari ko kuch nahin mila he
 a nurse said, "we do not provide food to any patient, there is no system for this
" (makasor praathmik swasthya centre ke baahar ek ambulance) Asha Devi's relatives deliver her food, but if they have to use the bathroom, they have to cross the dirty water and reach the only toilet, which is quite smelly

 Nawada DM Manoj Kumar is the top administrative officer of the area
 jab unke saamne aspataal kii samasyaon or dawaaon kii killat kii suchi rakhi jaati he, to vah kehete hai, main is maamle ko dekhuunga or uttardaayitv tay karuunga

 unhone kaha, in swasthya kendron par rojaanaa log aa rahe hai, or yah 10 saal pehle kii us sthiti se bilkul alag he, jab koi in kendron main aana nahin chahta tha, kyonki ye niskriy pade hue the

 poornima tithi, purnatv kii tithi maani jaati he
